2. Moderately Inaccurate

Being introverted and reserved typically means one tends to be more relaxed and at ease in social situations compared to someone who is extroverted. However, it's important to note that introversion does not equate to never feeling tense or nervous. Introverts might still experience anxiety or tension in certain situations, especially if they are in unfamiliar or overly stimulating environments. The statement "You can be tense" is moderately inaccurate because it implies a general state of tension which is not characteristic of introversion but rather an individual trait.
